## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: nonlinear oscillator dynamics
**Analysis**: This task involves modeling the acceleration (dv/dt) of a nonlinear harmonic oscillator as a function of position, velocity, and time. The equation of motion for such systems typically involves restoring forces (functions of x), damping terms (functions of v), and possibly driving forces (functions of t).

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Simple harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x (linear restoring force)
- Damped harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v (linear restoring + linear damping)
- Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 (cubic nonlinear restoring force)
- Damped Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v (cubic restoring + damping)
- Driven damped oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * sin(c3 * t) (with periodic driving)
- Driven Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v + c3 * cos(c4 * t) (driven nonlinear oscillator)
- Van der Pol oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * (1 - x**2) * v (nonlinear damping)
- Quintic nonlinearity: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x**5 (higher-order restoring force)
- Quadratic nonlinearity: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 (asymmetric restoring force)
- Nonlinear damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (cubic velocity damping)
- Coulomb-like friction: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v * (v**2)**0.5 (nonlinear friction model approximation)
- Position-velocity coupling: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x * v (mixed coupling term)
- Softening spring with damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v + c3 * x**2 * v (nonlinear spring and damping)
- Parametric oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x * (1 + c1 * cos(c2 * t)) (time-modulated stiffness)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Odd-power restoring forces (x, x**3, x**5) → symmetric potential wells preserving oscillation symmetry
- Even-power restoring forces (x**2) → asymmetric potential wells causing asymmetric oscillations
- Velocity-dependent terms proportional to v → energy dissipation or injection (damping/anti-damping)
- Terms like (1 - x**2)*v → amplitude-dependent damping causing limit cycle behavior (Van der Pol type)
- Sinusoidal or cosinusoidal functions of t → external periodic driving forces
- Cubic position terms x**3 → Duffing-type hardening (positive coefficient) or softening (negative coefficient) spring
- Products x*v or x**2*v → nonlinear damping that depends on displacement amplitude
- Absence of explicit time dependence → autonomous/conservative or dissipative system without external driving
- Linear superposition of x and v terms with no higher powers → system is in the linear regime near equilibrium
- Rational functions of x such as x/(1+c*x**2) → bounded restoring forces mimicking realistic spring saturation

- `x` (linear)

- The term `x*exp(-|x|)` is crucial and unusual

- No `t` dependence

Let me check candidates systematically. Most candidates lack `x*exp(-|x|)` or `v³`, so they won't match. I'll focus on candidates that could potentially match.

**Candidates with `v³`:** 35, 36, 39, 74, 83, 102, 103

**Candidate 35:** `c0*x + c1*x³ + c2*v + c3*v*x² + c4*v*|v|`
Note: `v*|v| = v²*sign(v)` which equals `|v|*v`. For v>0 this is v², for v<0 this is -v². This is NOT v³. No match.
Wait - actually v*|v| = |v|·v = v²·sign(v). And v³ = v²·v. These are the same thing! v*|v| = v·|v| and v³ = v·v². Since |v| ≠ v² in general, these are NOT the same. No match. Also missing x*exp(-|x|).

**Candidate 36:** `c0*x + c1*x³ + c2*v + c3*v*x² + c4*v*x⁴ + c5*v³`
Has v³ but also x³ and v*x⁴. Would need c1=0, c4=0. Then: c0*x + c2*v + c3*v*x² + c5*v³. Missing x*exp(-|x|). No match.

**Candidate 39:** `c0*x + c1*x³ + c2*v + c3*v*x² + c4*v³`
Set c1=0: c0*x + c2*v + c3*v*x² + c4*v³. Missing x*exp(-|x|). No match.

**Candidate 74:** `c0*x + c1*x³ + c2*v² + c3*v + c4*v*x² + c5*v*x⁴`
Has v² not v³. No match.

**Candidate 83:** `c0*x + c1*x³ + c2*v² + c3*v + c4*v*x²`
Has v² not v³. No match.

**Candidate 102/103:** Has sin() terms. sin cannot produce x*exp(-|x|). No match.
